				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Ich habe genug, BWV 82 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1727, revised 1731, 1735, 1747.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; </li><li>Aria (bass): Schlummert ein, ihr matten Augen (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li>Recitativo (bass): Mein Gott! wenn kömmt das schöne: Nun! (C&#160;minor)
